```markdown
# 113學年度辦理教師申請升等審查注意事項公告(含作業時程) ／公告日期:113.10.01

# Announcement ：Faculty Promotion Review Considerations (Including Operation Timeline) for Academic Year 2024

一、依據本校教師升等審查辦法、教師申請升等外審作業要點、教育部相關規定辦理。

二、本校專任教師其現職等級經教育部審定合格後，繼續服務，且符合本校「教師升等審查辦法」第二條各款之規定者，得向所屬學系(及同級)辦公室提出升等審查申請。

三、本校升等審查為預先審查制，申請人其現職等級年資計算至 114 年 7月 31日止，凡資格符合者，請於113年 11月 1日前依「元智大學教師申請升等應檢送資料檢查表」所列資料，向所屬學系(或同級)辦公室提出升等審查申請。

四、送審著作為送審教師取得現職等級教師資格後出版之專門著作、作品、成就證明、技術報告等方式，呈現其專業理論、實務或教學之研究或研發成果。

五、專門著作、作品、成就證明及技術報告等應符合下列各項規定之一：

(一)為已出版公開發行或經出版社出具證明將出版公開發行之專書。

(二)於國內外學術或專業刊物發表，或具正式審查程序，並得公開及利用之電子期刊，或經前開刊物，出具證明將定期發表。

(三)在國內外具有正式審查程序研討會發表，且集結成冊出版公開發行、以光碟發行或於網路公開發行之著作。

註：公開出版的相關說明：

1.在國內外具有正式審查程序研討會發表者，於送審時應檢附該論文集之出版頁（含出版者、發行人、發行日期…等）影本，始得送審。教師送審之專門著作(含代表著作、參考著作)請務必註明出版年月。

2.持國內外學術或專業刊物接受將定期發表之證明送審者，其代表著作應自該刊物出具證明所載日期起一年內發表，並自發表之日起二個月內，將該專門著作送交學校查核並存檔；其因不可歸責於申請者之事由，而未能於一年內發表者，至多以該著作出具接受證明之日起三年內為限。因可歸責於申請人未發表，或未於該刊物出具接受證明之日起三年內發表者，本校應駁回其申請，並報教育部撤銷其教師資格；其教師資格已審定合格發給教師證書，由本校報教育部廢止其教師資格，並追繳或註銷該等級之教師證書。

六、各學院應於 113年 11 月 5日前將「申請升等審查教師名冊彙整表」，經系(或同級)、院教評會審查，評分通過推薦者於114年 1月 8日前將應送審之資料送達人事室，以據憑辦理外審，逾期恕不受理。

(一)申請升等教師應於 113 年 11 月 5 日前繳交教育部乙式教師資格審查履歷表(書面及電子檔)予人事室，由人事室彙整送予研發處專責人員檢核確認送審之研究資料，繳交乙式教師資格審查履歷表之任何欄位資料有異動者，亦需同時通知人事室，若繳交予研發處檢核之研究資料與應送外審之研究資料有不符者，將取銷申請升等審查。

## 七、前項應送審資料包括（表單請至人事室/表單下載/教師升等下載）：

## (一)教師申請升等應檢送資料檢查表：

由每位申請升等教師填寫、自行檢核確認無誤後簽名，連同教師申請升等審查一覽表、教學、研究、輔導與服務等資料送學系(及同級)辦公室，辦理申請升等審查。

## (二)教師申請升等審查一覽表：

由送審教師依自選升等類型(學術領域、技術研發領域、教學實踐研究領域、文藝創作展演領域或體育競賽領域)填妥升等審查一覽表「壹、送審人基本資料」各欄位後，請以電子檔傳送給秘書室教師績效承辦人員核對，核對完成後，會協助列印書面並核章後，再送研發處承辦人填寫FWCI值，最後回給送審教師。

## (三)教師資格審查履歷表書面（乙式-外審用)：

1.請至「大專教師送審通報系統」(網址 https://www.schprs.edu.tw/wSite/ )填寫、列印(乙式)、存檔。教師經歷第一欄請填寫元智現職等級，任職時間至 114年7月。乙式教師資格審查履歷表請列印 2 份，1 份請裝訂於【升等研究資料】，1 份送系(及同級)辦公室。

2.教師資格審查履歷表之「英文姓名欄位」請確實填寫，英文姓名拼音請參護照或逕上外交部領事事務局網站查詢，國外學歷請同時填寫中英文校、系所、學位名。

(四)教師申請升等研究資料一式7份及提供電子檔之雲端空間連結網址（內附教育部乙式教師資格審查履歷表）。

(五)教師資格審查代表著作合著人證明 1份。(代表作無著合著人者，免附)

(六)著作／作品審查迴避參考名單 1份。

(七)教師申請升等教學及服務與輔導資料一式 2份。

(八)以著作(專門著作、技術報告、作品、體育成就證明及教學實踐研究)送審教師資格查核表。

(九)其他依法應檢附資料。

## 以上資料建議雙面印刷且暫不膠裝，經系院審查委員及人事室確認後再行裝訂送外審。

八、升等通過者，年資自 114年8月起生效。前項送審人檢附之審查資料，送審教師請務必確實檢查，如有不實或錯誤者，悉依教育部專科以上教師資格審定辦法第 44條規定辦理。  
九、113學年申請升等審查作業預定時程如附表，升等應檢附之表單請至人事室／表單下載／教師升等專區下載最新版本。

## 十、附表
```

#### OCR 25: files/教師升等/113學年度_教師申請升等審查注意事項公告_1130911定稿_英譯版.pdf

- OCR Markdown: /mnt/project/cache/ocr_completed_cache/ocr_md_assets/8b3b883680b3d177_113學年度_教師申請升等審查注意事項公告_1130911定稿_英譯版.md

```markdown
## for Academic Year 2024

The procedure shall be conducted in accordance with the “YZU Regulations for Evaluation of Faculty Promotion”, " YZU Guidelines for External Review of Faculty Promotion", and relevant regulations of the Ministry of Education.

2. Full-time faculty members whose current rank has been approved by the Ministry of Education and who continue their service, and meet the provisions of Article 2 of the ““YZU Regulations for Evaluation of Faculty Promotion” may submit an application for promotion review to the office of their affiliated department (or equivalent unit).

3. The university's promotion review is conducted as a pre-review system. The calculation of seniority for the applicant's current rank shall be up to July 31, 2025. Eligible applicants are required to submit their promotion review application and the relevant documents listed in the " Checklist for Yuan Ze University Faculty Promotion Application" to the office of their affiliated department (or equivalent unit) by November 1, 2024.

4. The submitted works for review shall include specialized publications, works, achievement certificates, technical reports, etc., published after the faculty member obtained their current rank, demonstrating their professional theoretical, practical, or teaching research or development achievements.

5. Specialized works, publications, achievement certificates, and technical reports must meet one of the following requirements:

(1). A monograph that has been published and publicly released or has been certified by the publisher to be published and publicly released.

(2). Published in domestic or international academic or professional journals, or in peerreviewed electronic journals that are publicly accessible and usable, or accompanied by certification from the aforementioned journals confirming scheduled publication.

(3). Published in domestic or international conferences with formal peer review processes, with works compiled into volumes for public release, distributed via CD, or published online.

Notes on public publication:

(1). For works presented at peer-reviewed domestic or international conferences, a copy of the publication page from the conference proceedings (including publisher, issuer, issue date, etc.) must be submitted for review. Faculty members must indicate the publication date of the specialized works submitted for review (including representative work and reference works).

(2). For works that have received a certification of acceptance for scheduled publication in an academic or professional journal, the representative work must be published within one year from the date indicated on the acceptance certification. The published work must be submitted to the school for verification and archiving within two months of publication. If, for reasons beyond the applicant’s control, the work cannot be published within one year, it must be published within three years from the date of the acceptance certification. If the delay in publication is attributable to the applicant, and the work is not published within three years, the university shall reject the application, and the Ministry of Education will revoke the applicant’s teaching qualification. If the qualification has already been approved and a teaching certificate issued, the university will report to the Ministry to annul the teaching qualification and revoke or cancel the teaching certificate at that level.

6. Each college shall submit the "Consolidated List of Teachers Applying for Promotion Review" by November 5, 2024. The list should be reviewed and approved by the departmental (or equivalent) and college-level Faculty Evaluation Committees. For those recommended with passing scores, the required documents must be submitted to the Personnel Office by January 8,

2025, for external review processing. Late submissions will not be accepted.

Faculties applying for promotion must submit a copy of the Ministry of Education's Teacher Qualification Review Resume Form (in both written and electronic formats) to the Personnel Office by November 5, 2024. The Personnel Office will compile the forms and forward them to the designated staff at the Research and Development Office for verification of the submitted research materials. If any section of the submitted resume is modified, the Personnel Office must be notified simultaneously. If discrepancies are found between the research materials submitted for verification and those intended for external review, the promotion review application will be revoked.

7. The materials required for the promotion review in the previous paragraph include the following (forms can be downloaded from the Personnel Office/Form Downloads/Teacher Promotion Downloads):

(1). Checklist for Yuan Ze University Faculty Promotion Application:

Each faculty applying for promotion must complete the checklist, verify the accuracy of the information, sign it, and submit it, along with the Faculty Promotion Review Checklist, and relevant materials for teaching, research, academic advice and other services, to the department (or equivalent) office for the promotion review application.

(2). Faculty Promotion Review Checklist:

The faculty applying for promotion should complete the relevant sections under "Basic Information of Applicant" on the overview form, based on their chosen promotion type (Academic Research Field, Technological Research and Development Field, Teaching Practice And Research Field, Cultural Or Artistic Creation And Exhibition Field, or Athletic Competition Field). The electronic version should be sent to the Secretariat Office staff responsible for faculty performance for verification. After verification, the staff will print the hard copy and affix the seal, then send it to the Office of Research and Development for the FWCI value entry, before returning it to the applicant.

(3). Teacher Qualification Review Resume Form (for external review): 【Ministry of EducationForm】

A. Fill out the form through the "Higher Education Faculty Submission Notification System" (Website: https://www.schprs.edu.tw/wSite/), print (external review form), and save it. For the first section of the teaching experience, indicate the current position at Yuan Ze University, with the employment period ending on July 31, 2025. Print 2 copies of the resume form, one to be bound with the 【Promotion Research Materials】, and one to be submitted to the department (or equivalent) office.

B. Ensure the "English Name" field is accurately completed. Use the passport as a reference for name spelling or check the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Consular Affairs Bureau website. For foreign degrees, provide the names of the school, department, and degree in both Chinese and English.

(4). Faculty Promotion Research Materials (7 copies) and a cloud link to electronic versions (with the Ministry of Education Teacher Qualification Review Resume External Review Form included).

(5). Yuan Ze University Faculty Promotion and Qualification Review Committee Certificate of Representative Publication and Coauthors (1 copy). (If the representative work has no co-authors, this is not required.)

(6). YZU Avoidance List of Publication Review Committee for Faculty Promotion (1 copy).

(7). Faculty Promotion Application relevant materials for teaching, academic advice and other services (2 copies).

(8). Teacher Qualification Verification Form (by publications, technical reports, creative works, sports achievement, or teaching practice and research report) 【Ministry of Education Form】 (9). Other required documents in accordance with the law.

For environmental reasons, it is recommended to print on both sides and avoid binding the materials until they are reviewed by the department and college committee members and confirmed by the Personnel Office. After confirmation, the materials can be bound and sent for external review.

8. Those who pass the promotion review will have their seniority effective from August 2025. The review materials submitted by the applicant must be carefully verified. Any false or erroneous information will be handled according to Article 44 of the Ministry of Education's Regulations on Regulations Governing Accreditation of Teacher Qualifications at Junior Colleges and Institutions of Higher Education.

9. The planned schedule for the promotion review process for the 2024 academic year is as shown in the attached table. The latest versions of the required forms for promotion applications can be downloaded from the Personnel Office / Form Downloads / Teacher Promotion section.

10. Attached Table
```

#### OCR 26: files/教師升等/113學年度升等作業簡報_1131004.pdf

- 關聯類型: 超連結（檔案）
- 本機檔案: admin/ho/files/教師升等/113學年度升等作業簡報_1131004.pdf

```markdown
# 113學年度教師升等說明會

## 2024 Academic Year Faculty Seminar on General Guidelines for Promotion

升等辦法 (Promotion Regulations)

多元升等 (Diverse Promotion)

類別說明 (Promotion Categories)

通過標準 (Passing Standards)

作業說明 (Procedure Guidelines)

Q&A

Speaker ：沈仰斌 主任(Director Yang-Pin Shen)Date : 2024/10/04

教師升等相關辦法(1/2)

Promotion Laws and Regulations

## 教育部(Ministry of Education)

教育人員任用條例(Act Governingthe Appointment of Educators) (2014.01.22)

專科以上教師資格審定辦法(Regulations Governing Accreditation of Teacher Qualifications at Junior Colleges and Institutions of Higher Education) (2023.08.30)

• 專科以上學校教師資格送審作業須知 (2024.08.12)

# 教師升等相關辦法(2/2)

Promotion Laws and Regulations

## 元智大學(Yuan Ze University)

校級(University-Leve)

• 教師升等審查辦法(YZU Regulations For Evaluation Of Faculty Promotion) (2022.11.02)

• 教師申請升等外審作業要點(YZU Guidelines For External Review Of Faculty Promotion) (2022.09.14)

• 教師教學暨輔導與服務成績考核辦法(YZU Regulations For Evaluating Faculty Performance In Teaching, Academic Advice And Other Services) (2024.07.10)

學院、系(及同級)(Colleges, Departments (And Equivalent)) 教師升等審查細則(Detailed Regulations For Faculty Promotion Review)

## 教師多元升等類別

## Diverse Promotion Categories

![](images/2ff91a552b3e52232f0dedfffd7499c928a1fb59a4fdfa55f91396e637a014ec.jpg)  
備註：教師得同時採取二種以上升等類型提出升等，以代表著作為判斷，如以學術研究之專門著作為代表作送審，仍得以技術報告、作品及成就證明為參考作，反之亦然。  
(Note: Teachers may simultaneously apply for promotion using two or more types of promotion categories. The representative work for evaluation could be an academic research publication. However, technical reports, creative works, and achievement proofs can also be considered as reference works, and vice versa.)

# 技術研發領域\_升等審查範圍

Scope Of Promotion Review In The Technological Research And Development Field

有關專利 技術移轉或創新之成果

(Achievements related to patents, technology transfer, or innovation.)

## 有關專業管理之個案研究全國性或國際性技術競賽獎項經整理分析具整體性及獨特見解貢獻之成果

(Case studies related to professional practice and management related case studies; awards won at national and/or international technology competition(s); results which have been organized and analyzed and contribute an integrated body of distinctive understandings.)

## 有關產學合作、技術應用及衍生成果或改善專案具有特殊貢獻之研發成果

(R&D results related to industry-academia cooperation,application(s) of technology; and/or derivative results and/or an improvement project that have made a distinct contribution.)

![](images/bcc607f3fd7cd9fea9bfe7b746c0072c341f8635be29568108e50e6936cf521a.jpg)

以「技術報告」送審教師資格

(Technical Reports Submitted For Teacher Accreditation Reviews)

# 技術研發領域升等\_整體之技術報告內容項目

# Overall Technical Report That Includes The Following MajorItems In The Technological Research And Development Field

# 教學實踐研究領域\_升等審查範圍

Scope Of Promotion Review In The Teaching Practice And Research Field

教師在課程设计教材教法教具科技媒体運用、評量工具運用等方式，採取適當之研究方法驗證成效之歷程，具有創新、改進或延伸應用之具體研究(发)成果，於校內外推广具有重要具體貢獻者，得以專門著作或技術報告送審。

(Faculties who have adopted appropriate research methods to verify the effectiveness of the process through curriculum design, teaching materials,teaching methods,teaching aids,applications of scientific and technological media, and the use of assessment tools, with specific research(development）results ofinnovation, improvement,or extendedapplication, andwhohave made significant and concrete contributions to the promotion of teaching on-campus and off-campus, may submit specialized publications or technical reports for an - accreditation review. )

# 教學實踐研究領域\_升等審查範圍

Scope Of Promotion Review In The Teaching Practice And Research Field

為推動多元升等，本部於105年5月25日修正審定辦法第21條第1項第1款規定，已將送審著作須具「…個人原創性，且非以整理、增刪、組合或編排他人著作而成之編著或其他非學術著作送審」修改為「…個人原創性，且非以整理、增刪、組合或編排他人著作而成之編著或其他非研究成果送審」放寬研究成果即可送審，爰國科會(科技部)補助人文學及社會科學經典譯註研究計畫成果，如符合上開要件，當可送審為代表作。

(教育部109年12月25 日台教高五字第1090172541 號函)

# 教學實踐研究領域升等教學實踐研究成果技術報告內容項目

# Submitted Results On Educational Practices Shall Be Accompanied By A Technical Report That Includes The Following Major Items

# 技術報告項目

Technical Report Items

1、教學實踐研究動機與主題 The motivation and theme of teaching practice research.

2、相關文獻探討 The related study documents.

3教學設計與研究方法 The teaching design and research methods.

4、研究成果及學生學習成效 R&D results and student's learning outcomes

5、方法或應用之創新及貢獻 The innovative aspects and result's contribution(s) of methods and applications.

## 教師升acloionceGulines)-a

## ➢ 按自選升等類別，整理自取得現職等級教師資格後公開出版或發表之研究表現與著作(含作品、成就證明及技術報告)。

(Research performance and works (academic writing, creative works, evidence of achievement, and technical reports) shall have been published or issued since obtaining the current teaching qualification.)

## 送審代表著作須為取得現職等級教師資格後所出版或為已接受且出具證明(接受函所載日期起一年內刊出或於升等生效日前刊出皆可)之著作。

(The submitted representative work for review must be either published after obtaining the current teaching position qualification or accepted with proof (published within one year from the date stated in the acceptance letter or published before the effective date of promotion).)

## ➢ 有送審人個人之原創性·且非僅以整理、增刪、組合或編排他人著作而成之編著或其他非研究成果著作。

(The works submitted for an accreditation review shall be the applicant's individual original work, and not simply produced by rearranging, adding to or deleting from, compiling, and/or editing the work(s) or other non-research results of any other person( s ) .)

## ➢ 與送審人任教科目性質相關。

(The nature of the representative work shall be related to the subject(s)taught by the applicant.)

## 研究資料意事ConsideationorRearchMatrials)

## 專門著作”出版“應符合下列規定之一：

(The academic writing shall be in one of the categories stipulated in the following subparagraphs:)

## ●為已出版公開發行或經出版社出具證明將出版公開發行之專書。

(Monographs already published and distributed or which have been accepted for publication and distribution by a publishing house which has issued a certificate to this effect.)

## ●於國內外學術或專業刊物發表，或具正式審查程序，並得公開及利用之電子期刊，或經前開刊物，出具證明將定期發表。

(Journal articles published in domestic and/or foreign scholarly journals or professional journals, or e-journals with a formal peer-review process and that may publish and use such articles, or articles that have been accepted for publication by a journal as just described, in which case the applicant shall submit documentary evidence that the journal will be issued within a fixed period.)

## ●在國內外具有正式審查程序研討會發表，且集結成冊出版公開發行、以光碟發行或於網路公開發行之著作。

(Papers that have been through a formal peer-review process included in proceedings of a domestic and/or overseas conference,and made public and distributed in the form of a volume, or CD, or online.)

教師資格審定（升等）未獲通過时，代表作得再次作为代表作提出申請，惟其整體著作需新增或更替一件以上·舉例如下：

● 案例1：原送審代表作A+參考作BCDE，送審未過時，得重新以代表作A+參考作 BCDF提出申請。

● 案例2：原送審代表作A+參考作BCD，送審未過時，代表作A+BCDE提出申請。

教師升業說明aculootionoedueGuidelines)

-研究資料意事(ConsidertionsorRearchMaterials)

期刊論文網路公開採認標準：因期刊電子化趨勢，部分期刊兼有網路及紙本之出版方式，或將已接受之論文，先於期刊網頁刊登發表再以紙本印刷，如具正式審查程序且得公開及利用者，皆符上開送審規定，其線上刊登日期與紙本出版日期不同時，得以送審人最有利原則從優認定·又網路刊登因期刊性質有公開存取（Open Access）或需透過付費或授權始能取得全文之形式，在合理範圍內皆屬可得公開利用情形。

O 二) 籌劃大型研討會演講藝文活動刊物編輯及入學考試。

。 (四) 參與行政服務，執行校務研究永續發展及社會責任專案相關計畫開設終身教育部課程等

O (六) 參與推廣教育班規劃及參加國際合作事務。

O (八) 輔導評量之學生問卷回饋意見。

O (十二) 對學生輔導工作有具體之措施

。 (十三) 協助學生解決問題，並與學務單位聯繫。

。 (十四) 參與有助於提昇本校聲譽之校外相關服務。

。 (十五)協助國內外招生活動參與校友服務。

## 學術領域\_專門著作(理工農醫)

(Academic Research Field - Academic Writing - Science, Engineering, Agriculture, Medicine)

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（甲表）

審查類別：學術領域\_專門著作(理工農醫)

審查編號：

![](images/40dec7653fff181e48e5420b9e9888cd1bb5ac2e50596b48f014613f9d805d32.jpg)

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（乙表）

審查评定基准：

1.教授：應在该学術领域内有獨特及持绩性著作並有重要具體之貢獻者。

2.副教授：應在该學街领域內有持绩性著作並有具体之貢獻者。

3.助理教授：應有相当於博士論文水准之著作並有獨立研究之能力者。

## 附注：

1.整理、增删、组合、编排他人著作而成之编著，或其他非研究成果著作，不得送赛。

2.送審代表作不得為學位論文或其論文之一部分。惟若未曾以該學位論文送審任一等級教師資格或属學位論文延續性研究送審者，經出版並提出说明，由專業審查認定著作具相當程度創新者，不在此限。

審查類別：學術領域\_專門著作(理工農醫）

3.為送審人取得前一職级至本次申请職级間之研究成果，得自行擇一為代表研究成果；其属系列之相關研究者，得合併為代表研究成果，至多五篇，其者列為参考研究成果。

112.06.21(111-08)校教師评審委會議修訂核備通過

審查编號：

![](images/500d61668687e8dd47c2d486c0783acd326f3e91040e30e8372997c9231d4498.jpg)

# 教師升說altooionoudline)- 外審審查意見表(External Review Evaluation Form)

## 學術領域\_專門著作(人文社會

(Academic Research Field - Academic Writing - Humanities and Social Sciences)

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（甲表）

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（乙表）

審查類別：學術領域專門著作（人文社會）

審查類別：學術領域\_專門著作(人文社會)

審查編號：

![](images/baa843994b2f3c4a70ded4306365989e82bb59ac806e10f1208e516fe07a84d6.jpg)  
審查评定基準：

1.教授：應在該學術领域内有獨特及持绩性著作並有重要具體之貢獻者。

2.副教授：應在该學術领域內有持绩性著作並有具體之貢献者。

3.助理教授：應有相當於博士論文水准之著作並有獨立研究之能力者。

附註：

1.整理、增删、组合、编排他人著作而成之编著，或其他非研究成果著作，不得送密。

2.送審代表作不得为學位論文或其論文之一部分惟若未曾以该學位論文送審任一等级教師責格或属學位論文延續性研究送審者，經出版並提出說明，由專業審查認定著作具相當程度創新者，不在此限。

3.为送審人取得前一職级至本次申请職级間之研究成果，得自行擇一为代表研究成果；其属系列之相關研究者，得合併为代表研究成果，至多五篇，其餘者列为参考研究成果。

112.06.21(111-08)校教師評審委會議修訂核備通過

![](images/b0f1fb92da4ff3f7da0af951715c84d506b86f342bd1492ae628ed69b9bafeac.jpg)

# 教師升作業說明FacltooiedureGuidelines)- 外審審查意見表(External Review Evaluation Form)

## 技術研究领域-技术報告

# (Technological Research and Development Field - Technical Reports)

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（甲表）

審查類別：技術研發領域-技術報告

審查编號：

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（乙表）

![](images/33510a5df186a7d9ab8872ce8d2ebce4f8e31e9d341ade081c238c754b97f5b4.jpg)  
審查评定基準：  
1.教授：持續從事學術、技術或實務研發，並應在该專業或產業及跨領域內有獨創及持績性著作或研發成果，且具有重要具體之貢献者。  
2.副教授：持續從事學術、技術或實務研發，並應在该專業或產業領域內有持績性著作或研發成果，且具有具體之貢献者：  
3.助理教授：持續從事學術、技術或實務研發，其研發成果貢獻良好並能顯示確實具有獨立研發之能力者。  
附注：  
1.整理、增删、组合、编排他人著作而成之编著，或其他非研究成果著作，不得送害。  
2.送審代表作不得为学位論文或其論文之一部分。惟若未曾以该學位論文送審任一等級教師资格或属學位論文延绩性研究送審者，經出版並提出說明，由專業審查認定著作具相當程度創新者，不在此限。  
3.为送審人取得前一職级至本次申请職级間之研究成果，得自行擇一為代表研究成果；其屋系列之相關研究者，得合併为代表研究成果，至多五篇，其餘者列为参考研究成果。

112.06.21(111-08)校教師評審委會議修訂核備通過

## 教學實踐研究領域-專門著作或技術報告

(Teaching Practice and Research Field - Special Book or Technical Reports)

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（甲表）

審查類別：教學實践研究領域□專門著作□技術報告審查編號：

![](images/80b2b64fb6e0e1bb91afafb29bd5b0d380cec0f0b9d66b94ee641c65eba0bb0d.jpg)  
審查评定基準：  
1.教授：應在任教学門领域内有獨創且持續性之教学實践研究成果，且教学成果良好，有具體推廣貢獻者。  
2.副教授：應在任教學門领域內有獨特之教學實践研究成果，且教學成果良好，有具體貢獻者。  
3.助理教授：應在任教學門领域內有優異之教學實践研究成果，持續從事教學實践研究，且教學成果良好者。  
附注：  
1.整理、增删、组合、编排他人著作而成之编著，或其他非研究成果著作，不得送害。  
2.送審代表作不得為學位論文或其論文之一部分。惟若未曾以该学位論文送審任一等級教師资格或属学位論文延績性研究送審者，經出版並提出说明，由專業審查認定著作具相當程度創新者，不在此限。  
3.为送害人取得前一職级至本次申请職级間之研究成果，得自行擇一为代表研究成果：其属系列之相關研究者，得合併为代表研究成果，至多五篇，其者列为参考研究成果。

# 專科以上學校教師資格審定辦法44條

# (Regulations Governing Accreditation of Teacher Qualifications at Junior Colleges and Institutions of Higher Education Article 44)

教師資格審查履歷表、合著人證明登載不實、代表作未確實填載為合著及繳交合著人證明、未適當引註未註明而重複發表、未註明其部分內容為已發表之成果或著作或其他違反學術倫理情事者：一年至五年不受理教師資格審定之申請。

著作、作品展演及技術報告有抄襲、造假、變造或舞弊情事：五年至七年不受理教師資格審查之申請。

學、經歷證件、成就證明、專門著作已為刊物接受將定期發表之證明、合著人證明為偽造、變造、以違法或不當手段影響論文之審查：七年至十年不受理教師資格審定之申請。

C 送審人或經由他人有請託、關說利誘、威脅或其他於擾審查人或審查程序情節嚴重：一年至二年不受理教師資格審定之申請。

送審人經檢舉或發現涉及上述各款之一情事者，不得申請撤回資格審查案，仍應依程序處理，且不受理審查期間為五年以上者，應同時副知各大專校院。

![](images/adc3fa96a6584563f09f56504e3fc2f3196910fb09139e6e8d43631cbd19ded7.jpg)  
Thank You For Your Participation

# 簡報內容歡迎至人事室網頁瀏覽
```

```markdown
# 114學年度辦理教師申請升等審查注意事項公告(含作業時程) ／公告日期:114.10.01

Announcement ：Faculty Promotion Review Considerations (Including Operation Timeline) for Academic Year 2025／Announcement date: October 1, 2025

一、依據本校「教師升等審查辦法」、本校「教師申請升等外審作業要點」、教育部相關規定辦理。

The procedure shall be conducted in accordance with the “YZU Regulations for Evaluation of Faculty Promotion”, " YZU Guidelines for External Review of Faculty Promotion", and relevant regulations of the Ministry of Education.

二、本校專任教師其現職等級經教育部審定合格後，繼續服務，且符合本校「教師升等審查辦法」第二條各款之規定者，得向所屬學系(及同級)辦公室提出升等審查申請。

Full-time faculty members whose current rank has been approved by the Ministry of Education and who continue their service, and meet the provisions of Article 2 of the “YZU Regulations for Evaluation of Faculty Promotion” may submit an application for promotion review to the office of their affiliated department (or equivalent unit).

三、本校升等審查為預先審查制，申請人其現職等級年資計算至 115年 7月 31日止，凡資格符合者，請於114年 10月 29日前依「元智大學教師申請升等應檢送資料檢查表」所列資料，向所屬學系(或同級)辦公室提出升等審查申請。

The university's promotion review is conducted as a pre-review system. The calculation of seniority for the applicant's current rank shall be up to July 31, 2026. Eligible applicants are required to submit their promotion review application and the relevant documents listed in the " Checklist for Yuan Ze University Faculty Promotion Application" to the office of their affiliated department (or equivalent unit) by October 29, 2025.

四、送審著作為送審教師取得現職等級教師資格後出版之專門著作、作品、成就證明、技術 報告等方式，呈現其專業理論、實務或教學之研究或研發成果。 The submitted works for review shall include specialized publications, works, achievement certificates, technical reports, etc., published after the faculty member obtained their current rank, demonstrating their professional theoretical, practical, or teaching research or development achievements.

五、專門著作、作品、成就證明及技術報告等應符合下列各項規定之一：

Specialized works, publications, achievement certificates, and technical reports must meet one of the following requirements:

(一) 為已出版公開發行或經出版社出具證明將出版公開發行之專書。

A monograph that has been published and publicly released or has been certified by the publisher to be published and publicly released.

(二) 於國內外學術或專業刊物發表，或具正式審查程序，並得公開及利用之電子期刊， 或經前開刊物，出具證明將定期發表。 Published in domestic or international academic or professional journals, or in peer-reviewed electronic journals that are publicly accessible and usable, or accompanied by certification from the aforementioned journals confirming scheduled publication.

(三) 在國內外具有正式審查程序研討會發表，且集結成冊出版公開發行、以光碟發行或於網路公開發行之著作。

Published in domestic or international conferences with formal peer review processes, with works compiled into volumes for public release, distributed via CD, or published online.

註：公開出版的相關說明：

Notes on public publication:

1. 在國內外具有正式審查程序研討會發表者，於送審時應檢附該論文集之出版頁（含出版者、發行人、發行日期…等）影本，始得送審。教師送審之專門著作(含代表著作、參考著作)請務必註明出版年月。

For works presented at peer-reviewed domestic or international conferences, a copy of the publication page from the conference proceedings (including publisher, issuer, issue date, etc.) must be submitted for review. Faculty members must indicate the publication date of the specialized works submitted for review (including representative work and reference works).

2. 持國內外學術或專業刊物接受將定期發表之證明送審者，其代表著作應自該刊物出具證明所載日期起一年內發表，並自發表之日起二個月內，將該專門著作送交學校查核並存檔；其因不可歸責於申請者之事由，而未能於一年內發表者，至多以該著作出具接受證明之日起三年內為限。因可歸責於申請人未發表，或未於該刊物出具接受證明之日起三年內發表者，本校應駁回其申請，並報教育部撤銷其教師資格；其教師資格已審定合格發給教師證書，由本校報教育部廢止其教師資格，並追繳或註銷該等級之教師證書。

For works that have received a certification of acceptance for scheduled publication in an academic or professional journal, the representative work must be published within one year from the date indicated on the acceptance certification. The published work must be submitted to the school for verification and archiving within two months of publication. If, for reasons beyond the applicant’s control, the work cannot be published within one year, it must be published within three years from the date of the acceptance certification. If the delay in publication is attributable to the applicant, and the work is not published within three years, the university shall reject the application, and the Ministry of Education will revoke the applicant’s teaching qualification. If the qualification has already been approved and a teaching certificate issued, the university will report to the Ministry to annul the teaching qualification and revoke or cancel the teaching certificate at that level.

六、各學院應於114年 11 月 4日前將「申請升等審查教師名冊彙整表」，經系(或同級)、院教評會審查，評分通過推薦者於115 年 1月 7日前將應送審之資料送達人事室，以據憑辦理外審，逾期恕不受理。

Each college shall submit the "Consolidated List of Teachers Applying for Promotion Review" by November 4, 2025. The list should be reviewed and approved by the departmental (or equivalent) and college-level Faculty Evaluation Committees. For those recommended with passing scores, the required documents must be submitted to the Personnel Office by January 7, 2026, for external review processing. Late submissions will not be accepted.

## (一) 申請升等教師應於 114 年 10 月 29 日前，E-mail「教育部乙式教師資格審查履歷表

(PDF電子檔)」予人事室，由人事進行初檢，繳交乙式教師資格審查履歷表之任何欄位資料有異動者，亦需同時通知人事室再進行複檢，以避免申請升等文件有誤，影響審查程序。

Faculties applying for promotion must email the "Ministry of Education Type B Faculty   
Qualification Review Resume (PDF electronic file)" to the Personnel Office by October 29,   
2025 for an initial review. If any changes are made to the submitted resume, the faculty   
member must notify the Personnel Office for a re-evaluation to ensure the accuracy of the   
promotion application documents and prevent any issues that may affect the review process.

## 七、 前項應送審資料包括（表單請至人事室/表單下載/教師升等下載）：

The materials required for the promotion review in the previous paragraph include the following (forms can be downloaded from the Personnel Office/Form Downloads/Teacher Promotion Downloads):

## (一) 教師申請升等應檢送資料檢查表：

Checklist for Yuan Ze University Faculty Promotion Application:

由每位申請升等教師填寫、自行檢核確認無誤後簽名，連同「教師申請升等審查一覽表」及「教師申請升等送審著作一覽表」(檢附每篇送審著作第一頁於本表後)，以及教學、研究、輔導與服務等資料送學系(及同級)辦公室，辦理申請升等審查。

Each faculty applying for promotion must complete the checklist, verify the accuracy of the information, sign it, and submit it, along with the Faculty Promotion Review Checklist, Faculty Promotion Review Checklist of Works(attach the first page of each submitted work after the form), relevant materials for teaching, research, academic advice and other services, to the department (or equivalent) office for the promotion review application.

## (二) 教師申請升等審查一覽表：

## Faculty Promotion Review Checklist:

由送審教師依自選升等類型(學術領域、技術研發領域、教學實踐研究領域、文藝創作展演領域或體育競賽領域)填妥升等審查一覽表「壹、送審人基本資料」各欄位後，請以書面或電子檔傳送給秘書室教師績效承辦人員核對，核對完成後，送回系(或同級)辦公室。

The faculty applying for promotion shall complete the "Section I: Basic Information of Applicant" on the Promotion Review Checklist Form according to their selected promotion category (Academic Research Field, Technological Research and Development Field, Teaching Practice and Research Field, Cultural or Artistic Creation and Exhibition Field, or Athletic Competition Field). The completed form shall be submitted—either in hard copy or electronic format—to the Secretariat staff responsible for faculty performance for verification. Once verified, the form will be returned to the department.

## (三) 教師申請升等送審著作一覽表：

Faculty Promotion Review Checklist of Works：

教師依個人自選升等類別(學術領域、技術研發領域、教學實踐研究領域、文藝創作展演領域或體育競賽領域)，填寫「教師申請升等送審著作一覽表」各欄後，並檢附每篇送審著作第一頁於本表後，請以書面或電子檔傳送給研發處承辦人員複核，複核完成後，送回系(或同級)辦公室。

The Faculty shall fill out all fields of the Promotion Review Checklist of Works based on their selected promotion category (Academic Research Field, Technological Research and Development Field, Teaching Practice and Research Field, Cultural or Artistic Creation and Exhibition Field, or Athletic Competition Field), and attach the first page of each submitted work to the form. The completed form shall be submitted, either in hard copy or electronic format, to the staff in charge at the Office of Research and Development for verification. Once verified, the form will be returned to the department.

## (四) 教師資格審查履歷表書面（乙式-外審用)：

Teacher Qualification Review Resume Form (for external review): 【Ministry of EducationForm】

1. 請至「大專教師送審通報系統」(網址 https://www.schprs.edu.tw/wSite/ )填寫、列印 (乙式)、存檔。教師經歷第一欄請填寫元智現職等級，任職時間至 115年 7月。乙 式教師資格審查履歷表請列印 2 份，1 份請裝訂於【升等研究資料】，1 份送系(及 同級)辦公室。 Fill out the form through the "Higher Education Faculty Submission Notification System" (website: https://www.schprs.edu.tw/wSite/), print (external review form), and save it. For the first section of the teaching experience, indicate the current position at Yuan Ze University, with the employment period ending on July 31, 2026. Print 2 copies of the resume form, one to be bound with the [Promotion Research Materials], and one to be submitted to the department (or equivalent) office.

2. 教師資格審查履歷表之「英文姓名欄位」請確實填寫，英文姓名拼音請參護照或逕 上外交部領事事務局網站查詢，國外學歷請同時填寫中英文校、系所、學位名。 Ensure the "English Name" field is accurately completed. Use the passport as a reference for name spelling or check the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Consular Affairs Bureau website. For foreign degrees, provide the names of the school, department, and degree in both Chinese and English.

(五) 教師申請升等研究資料一式7份及提供電子檔之雲端空間連結網址（內附教育部乙式教師資格審查履歷表）。Faculty Promotion Research Materials (7 copies) and a cloud link to electronic versions (withthe Ministry of Education Teacher Qualification Review Resume External Review Formincluded).

(六) 教師資格審查代表著作合著人證明 1份。(代表作無著合著人者，免附)

Yuan Ze University Faculty Promotion and Qualification Review Committee Certificate of Representative Publication and Coauthors (1 copy).   
(If the representative work has no co-authors, this is not required.)

(七) 著作／作品審查迴避參考名單 1份。

YZU Avoidance List of Publication Review Committee for Faculty Promotion (1 copy).

(八) 教師申請升等教學及服務與輔導資料一式 2份。

Faculty Promotion Application relevant materials for teaching, academic advice and other services (2 copies).

(九) 以著作(專門著作、技術報告、作品、體育成就證明及教學實踐研究)送審教師資格查核表。Teacher Qualification Verification Form (by publications, technical reports, creative works,sports achievement, or teaching practice and research report) 【Ministry of Education Form】  
(十) 其他依法應檢附資料。

Other required documents in accordance with the law.

以上資料建議雙面印刷且暫不膠裝，經系院審查委員及人事室確認後再行裝訂送外審。 For environmental reasons, it is recommended to print on both sides and avoid binding the materials until they are reviewed by the department and college committee members and confirmed by the Personnel Office. After confirmation, the materials can be bound and sent for external review.

八、升等通過者，年資自 115年8月起生效。前項送審人檢附之審查資料，送審教師請務必確 實檢查，如有不實或錯誤者，悉依教育部專科以上教師資格審定辦法第 44條規定辦理。 Those who pass the promotion review will have their seniority effective from August 2026. The review materials submitted by the applicant must be carefully verified. Any false or erroneous information will be handled according to Article 44 of the Ministry of Education's Regulations on Regulations Governing Accreditation of Teacher Qualifications at Junior Colleges and Institutions of Higher Education.

## 九、114學年申請升等審查作業預定時程如附表，升等應檢附之表單請至人事室／表單下載／教師升等專區下載最新版本。

The planned schedule for the promotion review process for the 2024 academic year is as shown in the attached table. The latest versions of the required forms for promotion applications can be downloaded from the Personnel Office / Form Downloads / Teacher Promotion section.
```

```markdown
# 114學年度教師升等說明會2025 Academic Year Faculty Workshop onGeneral Guidelines for Promotion

升等辦法 (Promotion Regulations)

多元升等 (Diverse Promotion)

類別說明 (Promotion Categories)

通過標準 (Passing Standards)

作業說明 (Procedure Guidelines)

Q&A

Speaker : 沈仰斌 主任(Director Yang-Pin Shen)Date : 2025/10/01

## 教師升等相關辦法(1/2)

Promotion Laws and Regulations

## 教育部(Ministry of Education)

教育人員任用條例(Act Governing the Appointment of Educators) (2014.01.22)

專科以上教師資格審定辦法(Regulations Governing Accreditation of Teacher Qualifications at Junior Colleges and Institutions of Higher Education) (2023.08.30)

專科以上學校教師資格送審作業須知 (2024.08.12)

# 教師升等相關辦法(2/2)

# Promotion Laws and Regulations

## 元智大學(Yuan Ze University)

校級(University-Leve )

• 教師升等審查辦法(Yuan Ze University Regulations for Evaluation of Faculty Promotion ) (2025.05.21)

• 教師申請升等外審作業要點(YZU Guidelines For External Review Of Faculty Promotion) (2025.09.10)

• 教師教學暨輔導與服務成績考核辦法(YZU Regulations For Evaluating Faculty Performance In Teaching, Academic Advice And Other Services) (2024.07.10)

學院、系(及同級)(Colleges,Departments (And Equivalent)) 教師升等審查細則(Detailed Regulations For Faculty Promotion Review)

## 教師多元升等類別

## Diverse Promotion Categories

![](images/d67b4724a4e1acf0a3bc273ae18d54f03773701e04c625e4234819224b3f2eb3.jpg)  
備註：教師得同時採取二種以上升等類型提出升等，以代表著作為判斷，如以學術研究之專門著作為代表作送審，仍得以技術報告、作品及成就證明為參考作，反之亦然。  
(Note: Teachers may simultaneously apply for promotion using two or more types of promotion categories. The representative work for evaluation could be an academic research publication. However, technical reports, creative works, and achievement proofs can also be considered as reference works, and vice versa.)

# 技術研發領域\_升等審查範圍

Scope Of Promotion Review In The Technological Research And Development Field

有關專利 技術移轉或創新之成果

(Achievements related to patents, technology transfer, or innovation.)

## 有關專業管理之個案研究全國性或國際性技術競賽獎項經整理分析具整體性及獨特見解貢獻之成果

(Case studies related to professional practice and management related case studies; awards won at national and/or international technology competition(s); results which have been organized and analyzed and contribute an integrated body of distinctive understandings.)

## 有關產學合作、技術應用及衍生成果或改善專案具有特殊貢獻之研發成果

(R&D results related to industry-academia cooperation,application(s) of technology; and/or derivative results and/or an improvement project that have made a distinct contribution.)

![](images/b99c6d5e6cc6c56538b6fae711d75668e24d236863b0c440a9a65617f6253707.jpg)

以「技術報告」送審教師資格

(Technical Reports Submitted For Teacher Accreditation Reviews)

# 技術研發領域升等\_整體之技術報告內容項目

# Overall TechnicalReport That IncludesThe FollowingMajorItems In The Technological Research And Development Field

![](images/e0e8645c18f614038b0500172d1911ce369eed9bbe04cbebff0a27cd7f538c61.jpg)

# 教學實踐研究領域\_升等審查範圍

Scope Of Promotion Review In The Teaching Practice And Research Field

教師在課程設計教材教法教具科技媒體運用、評量工具運用等方式，採取適當之研究方法驗證成效之歷程，具有創新、改進或延伸應用之具體研究(发)成果，於校內外推广具有重要具體貢獻者，得以專門著作或技術報告送審。

(Faculties who have adopted appropriate research methods to verify the effectiveness of the process through curriculum design, teaching materials,teaching methods,teaching aids,applications of scientific and technological media, and the use of assessment tools, with specific research(development）results ofinnovation, improvement,or extendedapplication, andwhohave made significant and concrete contributions to the promotion of teaching on-campus and off-campus, may submit specialized publications or technical reports for an - accreditation review. )

# 教學實踐研究領域\_升等審查範圍

Scope Of Promotion Review In The Teaching Practice And Research Field

為推動多元升等，本部於105年5月25日修正審定辦法第21條第1項第1款規定，已將送審著作須具「…個人原創性，且非以整理、增刪、組合或編排他人著作而成之編著或其他非學術著作送審」修改為「.個人原創性，且非以整理、增刪、組合或編排他人著作而成之編著或其他非研究成果送審」，放寬研究成果即可送審，爰國科會(科技部補助人文學及社會科學經典

譯註研究計畫成果，如符合上開要件，當可送審為代表作。

(教育部109年12月25 日台教高五字第1090172541 號函)

To promote diversifiedfaculty promotions, on May 25, 2016, the Ministry of Education revised Article 21, Paragraph 1, Subparagraph 1 of the Faculty Qualification Accreditation Regulations. The requirement that submission works must possess "originality and not be compilations or adaptations of others’works,such as edited collections or\_other non-academic works" was amended to "originality and notbe compilations or adaptations of others’works,such as edited collections or other nonresearch outputs." This relaxation allows\_research outputs to be eligiblefor review. Accordingly,outcomes of\_ the\_NSTC\_(formerly\_MOST)-funded\_projects on\_the annotated translation of classical works in the humanities and social sciences may be submitted as representative works if they meet the aforementioned requirements.

# 教學實踐研究領域升等教學實踐研究成果技術報告內容項目

# Submitted Results On Educational Practices Shall Be Accompanied By A Technical Report That Includes The Following Major Items

# 技術報告項目

Technical Report Items

1、教學實踐研究動機與主題 The motivation and theme of teaching practice research.

2、相關文獻探討 The related study documents.

3教學設計與研究方法 The teaching design and research methods.

4、研究成果及學生學習成效 R&D results and student's learning outcomes

5、方法或應用之創新及貢獻 The innovative aspects and result's contribution(s) of methods and applications.

# 文藝創作展演及體育競賽領域

# Cultural Or Artistic Creation And Exhibition Field and Athletic Competition Field

##

審查範圍及基準請詳參「專科以上教師資格審定辨法」(111.08.17）附表三

(Scope and Criteria for Teacher Accreditation Reviews, Please refer to Appendix 3)

體育競賽領域(Athletic Competition Field)

(Scope and Criteria for Teacher Accreditation Reviews, Please refer to Appendix 4)

## 教師升acloionceGudelines)-a

## ➢ 按自選升等類別，整理自取得現職等級教師資格後公開出版或發表之研究表現與著作(含作品、成就證明及技術報告)。

(Research performance and works (academic writing, creative works, evidence of achievement,and technical reports)shall have been published or issued since obtaining the current teaching qualification.)

## 送審代表著作須為取得現職等級教師資格後所出版或為已接受且出具證明(接受函所載日期起一年內刊出或於升等生效日前刊出皆可)之著作。

(The submitted representative work for review must be either published after obtaining the current teaching position qualification or accepted with proof (published within one year from the date stated in the acceptance letter or published before the effective date of promotion))

## ➢ 有送審人個人之原創性·且非僅以整理、增刪、組合或編排他人著作而成之編著或其他非研究成果著作。

(The works submitted for an accreditation review shall be the applicant's individual original work, and not simply produced by rearranging, adding to or deleting from, compiling, and/or editing the work(s) or other non-research results of any other person( s ) .)

## 與送審人任教科目性質相關

(Thenatureoftherepresentativeworkshallberelatedtothesubject(s)taughtbythe applicant.)

## 教師說cloneGlin

## 研究資料應注意事(ConsideationsforResearchMaterils)

## 專門著作”出版“應符合下列規定之一：

(The academic writing shall be in one of the categories stipulated in the following subparagraphs:)

## ●為已出版公開發行或經出版社出具證明將出版公開發行之專書。

(Monographs already published and distributed or which have been accepted for publication and distribution by a publishing house which has issued a certificate to this effect.)

## ●於國內外學術或專業刊物發表，或具正式審查程序，並得公開及利用之電子期刊，或經前開刊物，出具證明將定期發表。

(Journal articles published in domestic and/or foreign scholarly journals or professional journals, or e-journals with a formal peer-review process and that may publish and use such articles, or articles that have been accepted for publication by a journal as just described, in which case the applicant shall submit documentary evidence that the journal will be issued within a fixed period.)

## ●在國內外具有正式審查程序研討會發表，且集結成冊出版公開發行、以光碟發行或於網路公開發行之著作。

(Papers that have been through a formal peer-review process included in proceedings of a domestic and/or overseas conference,and made public and distributed in the\_form of a volume, or CD, or online.)

## 教師升作說alooeGine)-a

教師资格審定(升等)未獲通過時，代表作得再次作為代表作提出申請，惟其整體著作需新增或更替一件以上·舉例如下：

案例1：原送審代表作 A+參考作 BCDE，送審未過時，得重新以代表作A+参考作BCDF提出申請。

案例2：原送審代表作A+參考作BCD，送審未過時，代表作A+BCDE提出申請。

When the faculty qualification review (promotion) is not approved: A previously submited representative work may be resubmitted as a representative work for a new application. However, at least one other work must be added or replaced in the overall submission.

## Example 1:

Original submission: Representative work A + Supporting works B, C, D,E

New submission: Representative work A + Supporting works B, C, D, F

## ● Example 2:

Original submission: Representative work A + Supporting works B, C,D

New submission: Representative work A + Supporting works B, C, D, E

## 教師升業說明aclooinoceueGeline)-研

➢i: 期刊論文網路公開採認標準：因期刊電子化趨勢，部分期刊兼有網路及紙本之出版方式，或將已接受之論文，先於期刊網頁刊登發表再以紙本印刷，如具正式審查程序且得公開及利用者，皆符上開送審規定，其線上刊登日期與紙本出版日期不同時，得以送審人最有利原則從優認定・又網路刊登因期刊性質有公開存取（OpenAccess）或需透過付費或授權始能取得全文之形式，在合理範圍內皆屬可得公開利用情形。

(Criteria for Accepting Journal Articles Published Online for External Review : Due to the increasing trend of journal digitalization,some journals are published both online and in print, or may publish accepted articles on their websites prior to print publication. As long as the journal has a formal peer-review process and the article is publicly accessible and usable, it shall meet the requirementsfor external review submission.If the online publication date differs from the print publication date, the more favorable datefor theapplicant shall beadopted inaccordance with the principleof maximizing applicant benefit.In addition, depending on the nature of the journal, online publications may be in the form of Open Access or accessible only via subscription or licensing. As long as the content is reasonably available for public use,it shall be deemed acceptable.)

(教育部Ministryof Education 110年7月27日台教高(五)字第1100094494號函)

## 代表著作合著人證明 (1/2)

(Certificate of Representative Publication and Coauthors)

代表作係數人合著者，僅得由其中一人送審。送審人應以書面具體說明其參與部分，並由合著人簽章證明・前項合著人因故無法簽章證明時，送審人應以書面具體說明其參與部分，及無法取得合著人簽章證明之原因，經校級教評會審議同意者，得予免附。

(If the representative work has been co-authored by several people, only one of\_theco-authors maysubmit thatworkforanaccreditationreview. The applicant shall specify in writing the part(s)of the work in which they participated, and the other co-author(s)shall sign and certify the written statement. If a co-author is unable to provide the signed confirmation due to specific\_reasons,the\_applicant shall submit a written explanation detailing both their contribution and the reason the co-author's confirmation could not be obtained. Upon approval by the Faculty Evaluation Committee of School, the requirement for co-author confirmation may be waived.)

# 教師升業說明altooineGudelines)- 外審審查意見表(External Review Evaluation Form)

## 學術領域\_專門著作(理工農醫)

(Academic Research Field - Academic Writing - Science, Engineering, Agriculture, Medicine)

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（甲表）

審查類別：學術領域 專門著作(理工農醫）

審查編號：

![](images/6cff8f46db8e89519c574dc16f7d373b3d7241cf5f02ea0ae945fd228a9df82e.jpg)

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（乙表）

審查评定基准：

1.教授：應在该学術领域内有獨特及持绩性著作並有重要具體之貢獻者。

2.副教授：應在该學街领域內有持绩性著作並有具体之貢獻者。

3.助理教授：應有相当於博士論文水准之著作並有獨立研究之能力者。

審查類別：學術領域\_專門著作(理工農醫）

## 附注：

1.整理、增删、组合、编排他人著作而成之编著，或其他非研究成果著作，不得送赛。

2.送審代表作不得為學位論文或其論文之一部分。惟若未曾以该學位論文送審任一等級教師資格或属學位論文延續性研究送審者，經出版並提出说明，由專業審查認定著作具相當程度創新者，不在此限。

3.為送審人取得前一職级至本次申请職级間之研究成果，得自行擇一為代表研究成果；其属系列之相關研究者，得合併為代表研究成果，至多五篇，其者列為参考研究成果。

112.06.21(111-08)校教師评審委會議修訂核備通過

審查编號：

![](images/a772747e77d3bb9aeb7a02a49525a9348ac0d8478a4103546e11fbbb6b84ede8.jpg)

# 教師升業說明altooineGudelines)- 外審審查意見表(External Review Evaluation Form)

## 學術領域\_專門著作(人文社會

(Academic Research Field - Academic Writing - Humanities and Social Sciences)

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（甲表）

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（乙表）

審查類別：學術領域專門著作（人文社會）

審查類別：學術領域專門著作（人文社會）

審查編號：

![](images/540b8aa10479233094572cce087af2b03dfed59401f76d5cc358503d2c0c7e77.jpg)  
審查评定基準：

1.教授：應在該學術领域内有獨特及持绩性著作並有重要具體之貢獻者。

2.副教授：應在该學術领域內有持绩性著作並有具體之貢献者。

3.助理教授：應有相當於博士論文水准之著作並有獨立研究之能力者。

附註：

1.整理、增删、组合、编排他人著作而成之编著，或其他非研究成果著作，不得送密。

2.送審代表作不得为學位論文或其論文之一部分惟若未曾以該學位論文送審任一等级教師責格或属學位論文延續性研究送審者，經出版並提出說明，由專業審查認定著作具相當程度創新者，不在此限。

3.为送審人取得前一職级至本次申请職级間之研究成果，得自行擇一为代表研究成果；其属系列之相關研究者，得合併為代表研究成果，至多五篇，其餘者列为参考研究成果。

112.06.21(111-08)校教師評審委會議修訂核備通過

# 教師升說altooionoudline)- 外審審查意見表(External Review Evaluation Form)

## 技术研究领域-技术報告

# (Technological Research and Development Field - Technical Reports)

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（甲表）

審查類別：技術研發領域-技術報告

審查编號：

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（乙表）

![](images/1851eb4504fea3e34c928fc505323a374ea04e2b00e5a17158026cf6913d3244.jpg)  
審查评定基準：  
1.教授：持續從事學術、技術或實務研發，並應在该專業或產業及跨領域內有獨創及持績性著作或研發成果，且具有重要具體之貢献者。  
2.副教授：持續從事學術、技術或實務研發，並應在该專業或產業領域內有持績性著作或研發成果，且具有具體之貢献者：  
3.助理教授：持續從事學術、技術或實務研發，其研發成果貢獻良好並能顯示確實具有獨立研發之能力者。  
附注：  
1.整理、增删、组合、编排他人著作而成之编著，或其他非研究成果著作，不得送害。  
2.送審代表作不得为学位論文或其論文之一部分。惟若未曾以该學位論文送審任一等級教師资格或属學位論文延绩性研究送審者，經出版並提出說明，由專業審查認定著作具相當程度創新者，不在此限。  
3.为送審人取得前一職级至本次申请職级間之研究成果，得自行擇一為代表研究成果；其屋系列之相關研究者，得合併为代表研究成果，至多五篇，其餘者列为参考研究成果。

112.06.21(111-08)校教師評審委會議修訂核備通道

![](images/57e38781ed4e1e026506a80984530a6fb9c59c43eaa64d7825b5557e1e2c6b7c.jpg)

# 教師升業說明altooineGudelines)- 外審審查意見表(External Review Evaluation Form)

## 教學實踐研究領域-專門著作或技術報告

(Teaching Practice and Research Field - Special Book or Technical Reports)

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（甲表）

審查類別：教學實践研究領域□專門著作□技術報告審查編號：

![](images/67923233966593536c4e867bc35396847f6c78991b7d6655d40f85b3a591404e.jpg)  
審查评定基准：  
1.教授：應在任教学門领域内有獨創且持續性之教学實践研究成果，且教学成果良好，有具體推廣貢獻者。  
2.副教授：應在任教學門领域內有獨特之教學實践研究成果，且教學成果良好，有具體貢獻者。  
3.助理教授：應在任教學門领域內有優異之教學實践研究成果，持續從事教學實践研究，且教學成果良好者。  
附注：  
1.整理、增删、组合、编排他人著作而成之编著，或其他非研究成果著作，不得送害。  
2.送審代表作不得為學位論文或其論文之一部分。惟若未曾以该学位論文送審任一等級教師资格或属学位論文延績性研究送審者，經出版並提出说明，由專業審查認定著作具相當程度創新者，不在此限。  
3.为送害人取得前一職级至本次申请職级間之研究成果，得自行擇一为代表研究成果：其属系列之相關研究者，得合併为代表研究成果，至多五篇，其者列为参考研究成果。

112.06.21(111-08)校教師評審委會議修訂核備通過

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（乙表）

![](images/549255f017124f60fd9a9e389f7aac7f187bccb44704a61feadb1220befdefec.jpg)

![](images/8e9f9aa2c739b1bbf2b3a259278b1739b46393c89a5feae5d6662aeafe1cefae.jpg)

審查评定基準：

# 教師升業說明altooineGudelines)- 外審審查意見表(External Review Evaluation Form)

## 文艺創作展演領域作品及成就-艺術-設計

(Works and Achievements - Arts - Design)

元智大學教師升等審查意見表（甲表）

審查類別：作品及成就-藝術-設計

審查編號：

![](images/17bb234f30a25b082a8cfb97f6648b760fa655e9c2c26d9029c98484e5358791.jpg)

1.教授：應在该學術领域内有獨特及持續性作品並有重要具體之貢獻者。

2.副教授：應在该學街领域内有持绩性作品並有具體之貢献者。

3.助理教授：應有相當於博士水准之創作作品。

附注：为送害人取得前一職级至本次申请職级間之研究成果，得自行择一为代表研究成果：其属系列之相關研究者，得合併为代表研究成果，至多五篇，其餘列为参考研究成果。

112.06.21(111-08)校教師評審委會議修訂核備通過

## 元智大學教師升等審查意見表（乙表）

審查類别：作品及成就-藝術-設計

審查編號：

![](images/eed150e09a34eaf449b209937409a56c57d6199419144f39047311a9f27fa696.jpg)

# 專科以上學校教師資格審定辦法44條

# (Regulations Governing Accreditation of Teacher Qualifications at Junior Colleges and Institutions of Higher Education Article 44)

教師資格審查履歷表、合著人證明登載不實、代表作未確實填載為合著及繳交合著人證明、未適當引註未註明而重複發表、未註明其部分內容為已發表之成果或著作或其他違反學術倫理情事者：一年至五年不受理教師資格審定之申請。

著作、作品展演及技術報告有抄襲、造假、變造或舞弊情事：五年至七年不受理教師資格審查之申請。

學、經歷證件、成就證明專門著作已為刊物接受將定期發表之證明、合著人證明為偽造、變造、以違法或不當手段影響論文之審查：七年至十年不受理教師資格審定之申請。

C 送審人或經由他人有請託、關說利誘、威脅或其他於擾審查人或審查程序情節嚴重：一年至二年不受理教師資格審定之申請。

送審人經檢舉或發現涉及上述各款之一情事者，不得申請撤回資格審查案，仍應依程序處理，且不受理審查期間為五年以上者，應同時副知各大專校院。

![](images/0d0aa22649aacb8f6637955453ffdcd9d9ba1c0b6e128cfa774935b9448e7c7b.jpg)  
Thank You For Your Participation

# 簡報內容歡迎至人事室網頁瀏覽

# Welcome to be Browsed the PPT on the Personnel Office's Webpage.
```

```markdown
## 升等著作將發表證明文件

## Proof of Forthcoming Publication for Promotion-Related Works

• 送審著作將發表證明(選)：如期刊接受函、書籍出版日通知等。

Documentary Proof of Upcoming Publication of the Work Under Review (Optional)：e.g., letter of acceptance from a journal, notification of scheduled book publication, etc.

※註：持國內外學術或專業刊物接受將定期發表之證明送審者，其代表作應自該刊物出具接受證明之日起一年內發表，並自發表之日起二個月內，將該專門著作送交學校人事室查核並存檔；其因不可歸責於送審人之事由，而未能於一年內發表者，至多以該刊物出具接受證明之日起三年內為限。

If the applicant submits evidence for an accreditation review that their representative work has been accepted for publication within a definite period by a domestic or foreign scholarly journal or professional journal, the representative work shall be published within one year from the date that the journal issued its letter of acceptance or similar notification, and the applicant shall submit a copy of the academic work to the Institution Personnel Office for checking and filing within two months after the work is published. If for some reason（s） not attributable to the applicant the work is not able to be published within that one year, the maximum possible extension period is three years from the date that the journal issued its original letter of acceptance or similar notification.

![](images/98ec74fe27ea0832396f39bc245db96bc9783f7e0c55f1156daf686a3ddb13ae.jpg)
```
